Resume
You're standing in a small one room office. It's pretty sparse with a shabby desk buried under piles of paper and various knick-knacks, an uncomfortable looking wooden chair, a bookshelf, and a few pictures hanging on the wall.\n\nThe only door out is fitted with an old-fashioned mail slot. And it's locked.\n\n"Excuse me?" comes a muffled voice from the other side of the door. "Could you help me? I'm supposed to apply to this big job with <b>Local Marketing Inc.</b>, but I some how locked myself out of the office. All the pieces to my resume are in there with you, just collect them and stuff them through this slot. Ok?"\n\n[[Sure (Not that I have much choice.)|desk]]

You start to shuffle through the stack of papers and doodles piled on the desk looking for anything that resembles a resume.\n\nWhen a [[scrap of paper|objective statement]] falls to the floor you reach down and pick it up.

"Great! I'd start with the [[desk|desk2]], I'm pretty sure I left something over there."\n\n\n\n
The bookshelf is stuffed with different kinds of books. You pick up a [[big, red one |ahs]] first.
Cory Olesen\nStoryteller, writer, occasional puppy wrangler
<<set $visited_door = "3">>\nYou dust off on the pictures on the wall. One is a diploma with gilded edges and written in pompous old-style script that reads:\n\n<center>Bachelor of Arts - English, Creative Writing\nGeorgia College & State University\n2006 - 2010</center>\n\nYou carefully take the diploma from the wall and slide it through the [[slot|door]].\n\n<<playsound "MC2.mp3">>\n\n
